We have been serving the community in Queenstown, Holland, Bukit Merah and neighbouring towns since 1967. Located on level 2 of Faith Methodist Church, we offer Full-day Programme from 7am - 7pm on weekdays for children aged 18 months (Playgroup) to 6 years old (K2) in a conducive learning environment that inspires purposeful and joyful learning. Our holistic STEM-based and technology-infused curriculum encourages children to explore and make discoveries as they engage the learning corners specially designed for each level. <div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.18s;" class="preSlide"><em>Principal’s Message</em></h2><p class="sqsrte-large preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.186s;"><strong>MRS PAULINE CHIA</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.192s;">Hello! I’m Pauline, the principal of Faith Methodist Preschool (FMP). This preschool is close to my heart because I was once a student here and it’s an honour to be back to serve!</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.198s;">Established in 1967, this preschool has been serving the community for more than 50 years. Therefore, our theme verse this year is ‘Give thanks to the Lord for His steadfast love endures forever.’ It is taken from 2 Chronicles 20:21b. We believe that it is only by the grace of God that we are placed in this neighbourhood for a purpose to serve families.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.204s;">At FMP, aside from the wonderful programmes we have in enriching the child’s learning, we believe in nurturing the character of children as a crucial part of their developmental journey. It is said : It takes a village to raise a child. We believe in connecting with parents, community and the church in supporting every child’s holistic development.  We place emphasis in and are dedicated to work closely with parents to nurture our children because we believe that parents play a very important role in their lives.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.21s;">Come! Visit our school and get to know us better. We are conveniently located next to Commonwealth MRT station. </p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></div>
    </div>
  
  </div>

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h2 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.276s;" class="preSlide">Special<br>Programmes.</h2>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-86efaec7b4c7e76de7b6"><div class="sqs-block-content"><article class="c-tabs__wrapper"><div class="c-tabs has-hover"><ul class="c-tabs__tablist"><li><a class="c-tabs__tab" aria-selected="true" aria-controls="tabpanel--values-in-action-learning" id="tab--values-in-action-learning" Learning</span></a></li><li><a class="c-tabs__tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--community-outreach-projects-" id="tab--community-outreach-projects-" data-preserve-html-node="true"> Projects </span></a></li></ul><div class="c-tabs__content"><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="true" aria-controls="tabpanel--values-in-action-learning" Learning</span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--values-in-action-learning" id="tabpanel--values-in-action-learning"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1630902128345_9794"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.282s;">Values and Character education is an integral part of our curriculum at Faith Methodist Preschool. Each class does a mini project to apply values learnt (e.g. saving the earth, civic mindfulness, Christian values, etc) into action at the end of every term. Participation in such values-in-action initiatives provides opportunities for our children to put the values that they learn in our daily curriculum to meaningful and authentic action.</p>
</div>




















  
  



</div></div></div></div></section><a class="c-tabs__accordion-tab" aria-selected="false" aria-controls="tabpanel--community-outreach-projects-" id="tab--community-outreach-projects-" href="#tabpanel--community-outreach-projects-" aria-expanded="false" style="display: none;"><span class="c-tabs__tab-title"><img data-preserve-html-node="true" src="https://static1.squarespace.com/static/5fe9e26f8d20536a3fc01415/t/610a490c7244840303583aaf/1628064012412/Group+67.png" alt="" title="" width="60" height="60"> Community Outreach <br data-preserve-html-node="true"> Projects </span></a><section class="c-tabs__tabpanel" aria-labelledby="tab--community-outreach-projects-" id="tabpanel--community-outreach-projects-" style="display: none;"><div class="c-tabs__tabpanel-inner"><div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" data-border-radii="{&quot;topLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;topRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomLeft&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0},&quot;bottomRight&quot;:{&quot;unit&quot;:&quot;px&quot;,&quot;value&quot;:0.0}}" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1630902128345_12386"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.288s;"><strong>We organise Values In Action for our preschoolers annually as a platform for them to put values that we teach in school into meaningful action to reach out to and serve the community, especially those who are less privileged. We also invite parents to collaborate with us in our Values in Action projects.</strong></p>
</div>

When he first transferred to Faith Methodist Preschool, he initially built walls around himself due to his dislike for schooling from the unpleasant experiences in his previous school. After he engaged Mrs Chia and experienced the positive classroom environment in his FMP K1 class, he started to enjoy going to school a lot more and has improved his social and interpersonal skills significantly. It is also a big plus that the school has a structured yet enjoyable curriculum that seems to help him be more P1 ready than many of his peers from other preschools during playdates.  </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.324s;">Special shout out to N1 teachers as well, for helping my second child enjoy school and becoming very bonded to his teachers and classmates. We are satisfied with the broad, yet rigorous curriculum offered by the school and pleased to see him develop a keen interest in music. </p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.33s;"><em>— Parents of  Say Xian Yi and Xian Kun</em></p></div>

            sectionBackground.style.top = '';

<!-- Add Section IDs for anchor links -->
<script>
(function () {
  window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    var sections = document.querySelectorAll('section');
    var windowPath = window.location.pathname;
    // If page is set to homepage then set the anchor to home. i.e. #home-1
    if (windowPath === '/') {
      windowPath = 'home';
    }

    var anchorID = windowPath.replace('/', '');

    sections.forEach((section, i) => {
      section.id = `${anchorID}-${i+1}`;
    })
  })
})()
</script>

<script>
window.onscroll = function() {myFunction()};

function myFunction() {
  var winScroll = document.body.scrollTop || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  var height = document.documentElement.scrollHeight - document.documentElement.clientHeight;
  var scrolled = (winScroll / height) * 100;
  document.getElementById("progressBar").style.width = scrolled + "%";
}
</script>
